| 0:07:42| This is a proclamation to publicly recognize women in public office.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=462)|
| 0:07:49| And it reads, whereas the month of March is Women's History Month| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=469)|
| 0:07:53| and celebrates the significant contributions women of all races, ethnicities,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=473)|
| 0:07:58| and backgrounds have made to the world,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=478)|
| 0:08:00| and whereas women play a critical role in the vitality and diversity of our communities| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=480)|
| 0:08:05| and are essential to ensuring Knox County is well represented,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=485)|
| 0:08:08| and whereas while the 20th century was a pivotal time of growth for women entering politics,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=488)|
| 0:08:14| women remain underrepresented in male-dominated fields,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=494)|
| 0:08:18| and thus providing opportunities to support women in public office is imperative,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=498)|
| 0:08:22| and whereas recognizing women in public office will bring awareness to the fundamental necessity of their work| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=502)|
| 0:08:28| and will inspire other young people to serve their communities.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=508)|
| 0:08:32| Now, therefore, I, Glenn Jacobs,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=512)|
| 0:08:34| Knox County Mayor, do hereby proclaim tomorrow, May 19th, 2019,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=514)|
| 0:08:38| as Women in Public Office Day in Knox County| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=518)|

| 1:33:12| Unfortunately, what they are is it's a covenant for maintenance for permanent stormwater facilities.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=5592)|
| 1:33:20| What those typically are, what you see is detention basins, swells, and things like that.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=5600)|

| 1:33:33| they're required to execute this document.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=5613)|
| 1:33:36| It gives us the right to ensure that those devices, detention basins, swells,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=5616)|
| 1:33:41| and any of those engineered best management practices are maintained by the landowners in perpetuity.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=5621)|
| 1:33:49| If the landowner chooses not to do that, it also gives us the right to go upon that property to ensure that the safety,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=5629)|
| 1:33:56| welfare, and safety of the public is taken care of.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=5636)|

| 1:49:10| You've got 10 minutes, Ms. Testerman.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6550)|
| 1:49:15| Thank you, Chairman Neistrom and esteemed Commissioners.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6555)|
| 1:49:19| I appreciate your time on this.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6559)|
| 1:49:21| I should be under five minutes, and this is our shelter medical director,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6561)|
| 1:49:26| which should also be under five minutes.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6566)|
| 1:49:31| I'm here tonight supporting a proposed ordinance to institute a community cat diversion program| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6571)|
| 1:49:36| that will directly and significantly impact the overpopulation of free-roaming cats.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6576)|
| 1:49:42| Community cat diversion has been proven to be successful in more than 650 jurisdictions around the country.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6582)|
| 1:49:47| And we are, in fact, the largest county in the state of Tennessee,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6587)|
| 1:49:51| not practicing the only proven best practice of population control through a comprehensive program| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6591)|
| 1:49:56| to include shelter, neuter, vaccinate, return, trap, neuter, vaccinate, return,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6596)|
| 1:50:01| outreach and conflict resolution.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6601)|
| 1:50:04| This is not just about decreasing the intake of cats into the shelter.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6604)|
| 1:50:07| This is about solving a community issue through spay-neuter practices| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6607)|
| 1:50:12| and is the single best solution to both significantly reducing the overall population of free-roaming cats| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6612)|
| 1:50:18| and decreasing the impact on the ecosystem as well as the wildlife population.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6618)|
| 1:50:23| This issue is not whether free-roaming cats can have negative impacts.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6623)|
| 1:50:27| The issue is how we can lower their numbers and reduce whatever negative impacts there are.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6627)|
| 1:50:32| Over the last three years at Young-Williams, we took in 8,735 cats.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6632)|
| 1:50:37| Of that, only 381 or 4% were reunited with an owner.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6637)|
| 1:50:43| Of that 8735, 3381 were euthanized.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6643)|
| 1:50:48| That's 39%.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6648)|
| 1:50:50| A trapping-euthanized approach simply doesn't work.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6650)|
| 1:50:54| The rate of reproduction of cats is so significant that there will never be a point of which,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6654)|
| 1:50:59| through a euthanasia method, the cat population will decrease but instead is shown to increase.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6659)|
| 1:51:04| And given the birth rate of humans at 10,000 a day and cats and puppies at 70,000 a day,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6664)|
| 1:51:11| there simply will never be enough homes for these animals,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6671)|
| 1:51:15| lest we take great strides in practicing sterilization.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6675)|
| 1:51:20| We'd love for all cats to be kept inside, absolutely,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6680)|
| 1:51:24| educate and promote responsible pet ownership to adopters when they come to our facility.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6684)|
| 1:51:29| Unfortunately, indoor cats is not a reality,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6689)|
| 1:51:32| and an enormous number of community cats are not owned and are cared for by multiple people.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6692)|
| 1:51:38| By returning these cats to their place of origin,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6698)|
| 1:51:41| friendly neighborhood cats have a 70% to 100% chance of finding their way back home| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6701)|
| 1:51:46| and being reunited with their owner or owners.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6706)|
| 1:51:50| While there hasn't been a reported cat case of rabies in Knox County since 1969,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6710)|
| 1:51:55| public health remains of utmost concern for us.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6715)|
| 1:51:58| As part of this program, all cats would be released back to their original habitat,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6718)|
| 1:52:03| having been rabies vaccinated and dewormed, sending them back healthier than when they came in.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6723)|
| 1:52:08| This will increase community immunity, decrease the number of community cats,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6728)|
| 1:52:13| and end the use of euthanasia for population control of cats in a shelter.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6733)|
| 1:52:18| A position statement by the American Public Health Association| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6738)|
| 1:52:21| and its Veterinary Public Health Special Interest Group,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6741)|
| 1:52:25| which focuses on preventing the spread of zoonotic diseases from animals to people,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6745)|
| 1:52:29| such as rabies and taxoplasmosis, states,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6749)|
| 1:52:32| we encourage communities to discuss trap-neuter-return as a management practice| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6752)|
| 1:52:38| to control community cats and to adopt this practice where possible.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6758)|
| 1:52:42| The American Bar Association and International Association of City and County Managers| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6762)|
| 1:52:46| have also issued similar position statements.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6766)|
| 1:52:50| Even trap-and-remove is completely ineffective,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6770)|
| 1:52:53| as that's also been what shelters have practiced for decades.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6773)|
| 1:52:57| We are expending resources.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6777)|
| 1:52:59| We are wasting taxpayer dollars by holding cats,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6779)|
| 1:53:02| treating them for shelter-related stress and illnesses like upper respiratory infection,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6782)|
| 1:53:07| which often leads to euthanasia.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6787)|

| 1:55:18| which is that trap-and-remove and euthanize does not work.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6918)|
| 1:55:22| It's ineffective in reducing the number of feral cats in the community,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6922)|
| 1:55:25| and stray cats in the community, it's a waste of time and money for the community.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6925)|
| 1:55:30| Cats are there because there's something to eat.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6930)|
| 1:55:33| There's shelter. There's food. There's water.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6933)|
| 1:55:35| There's a reason that they're there.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6935)|
| 1:55:37| So merely taking them away is a temporary fix,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6937)|
| 1:55:40| and animal control officers will tell you if they trap out a group of cats within six months, more will come.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6940)|
| 1:55:47| It's because there's something there.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6947)|
| 1:55:49| Since we can't get rid of all the potential food sources for cats in the community,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6949)|
| 1:55:53| I think it's better to focus on sterilization.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6953)|
| 1:55:57| Without sterilization or return, new cats move in.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6957)|
| 1:56:00| TNVR returns cats to where they came from.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6960)|
| 1:56:03| Now they're vaccinated and healthier, and they can continue to occupy that environment.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6963)|
| 1:56:08| Yes, if there's places where they're not welcome, you can use deterrents to help usher them away.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6968)|
| 1:56:14| But trap-and-remove and euthanize is reactive,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6974)|
| 1:56:18| and sterilization that we're proposing is proactive and preventative.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6978)|
| 1:56:22| According to the Million Cat Challenge, I think Janet's already mentioned,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6982)|
| 1:56:25| many communities have adopted this.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6985)|
| 1:56:27| The only thing they say is, we wish we'd done it sooner.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6987)|
| 1:56:31| In 2007, Young-Williams launched the Spay Shuttle to remove all barriers to spay and neuter for our community,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6991)|
| 1:56:38| thanks to the help of many organizations and grants.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=6998)|
| 1:56:42| This program has resulted in significant decline in shelter intake.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=7002)|
| 1:56:46| We have essentially reached a plateau with cat intake,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=7006)|
| 1:56:49| and that's because cats are just amazing survivors.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=7009)|
| 1:56:53| One female cat can have up to three litters with an average of six kittens in each litter in a single season.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=7013)|
| 1:56:59| The first litter can start having its own litter before the end of that breeding season.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=7019)|
| 1:57:04| So it's easy to see how you can go from one cat to 20 very quickly.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=7024)|
| 1:57:10| So sterilization is the way to kind of just nip that in the bud.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=7030)|
| 1:57:15| Some people express a concern that TNR is irresponsible pet ownership.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=7035)|

| 2:22:59| If you would, explain how the bonding is so much better.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=8579)|
| 2:23:03| Yeah, and I can send Drusilla a YouTube video| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=8583)|
| 2:23:07| because it's probably the best way to get a feel for it.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=8587)|
| 2:23:09| But it's essentially a propane heater that comes down| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=8589)|
| 2:23:14| and actually heats up the asphalt surrounding the pothole,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=8594)|
| 2:23:17| and you mix in fresh asphalt with it.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=8597)|
| 2:23:21| And then once it's heated up and pliable,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=8601)|
| 2:23:24| you break it in and then actually have a roller and compact it.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=8604)|
| 2:23:28| So it essentially prevents the cracks and the seams| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=8608)|
| 2:23:32| because what's causing that pothole is water.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=8612)|
| 2:23:34| So by heating it up and sealing those joints,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=8614)|
| 2:23:37| you don't have the potential for water getting back into the asphalt pavement.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=8617)|
| 2:23:40| But I'll send a YouTube link to Drusilla so she can forward it.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=8620)|
| 2:23:44| It's a relatively new technique,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=8624)|
| 2:23:46| and it's a much more effective way of repairing a pothole long-term.| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=8626)|
| 2:23:50| Yeah, I think you said earlier that a lot of times an initial pothole will form,| [source video](https://archive.org/details/CoComWSR1467190318?start=8630)|
